In particular, the hypotheses of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-vector-seed} are automatic
on any realized spectral vector-line locus (the completed vector seed
and its spectral-shift action are canonically transported from the
standard quantum-loop evaluation line).
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
Conjugation by the vector-line equivalence defines
\(\mathsf{T}^{\omega}_a\) on \(\mathcal{L}^{\mathrm{vec}}_{q}\),
and the group law and unit transport from
Proposition~\ref{prop:quantum-fd-vector-seed-shifts} by conjugation.
\end{proof}

\begin{proposition}[On the realized spectral vector-line locus, loop
rotation descends to the full spectral compact core;
\ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-core-shifts}
Work in the setting of
Propositions~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-seed-shift-construction}
and~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-realization-formal}. Assume that
the exact braided monoidal functor \(J_q^\omega\) restricts to an
equivalence
\[
\mathcal{L}^{\mathrm{vec,fd}}_{q}\xrightarrow{\sim}
\mathcal{L}^{\mathrm{vec}}_{q}.
\]
Let \(\mathsf{T}^{\omega}_a\) be the induced exact braided-monoidal
autoequivalences of the completed vector line from
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-seed-shift-construction}.
Then each \(\mathsf{T}^{\omega}_a\) extends uniquely to an exact
braided-monoidal autoequivalence, still denoted
\[
\mathsf{T}^{\omega}_a\colon
\mathcal{C}_q^\omega\xrightarrow{\sim}\mathcal{C}_q^\omega,
\]
and these extensions preserve the completed vector packet, completed
fundamental packet, and completed tensor-generator packet. In addition,
\[
\mathsf{T}^{\omega}_{a+b}\cong
\mathsf{T}^{\omega}_a\circ \mathsf{T}^{\omega}_b,
\qquad
\mathsf{T}^{\omega}_0\cong \id
\]
on the full spectral compact core.
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
Each \(\mathsf{T}^{\omega}_a\) is exact and braided monoidal on the
completed vector line
(Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-seed-shift-construction}),
hence preserves the ordered vector packet, the completed fundamental
packet (by
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-vector-packet}), and the
tensor-generator packet. Since
\(\mathcal{C}_q^\omega=
\operatorname{thick}^{\mathrm{idemp}}(\mathcal{G}^{\mathrm{fund}}_{q})\),
uniqueness of thick-closure extension gives the autoequivalence of
\(\mathcal{C}_q^\omega\) and transports the group law.
\end{proof}

\begin{proposition}[Factorization-locus specializations:
\texorpdfstring{$\rho_a$}{rho\_a} pullback, core from vector line,
seed-line forcing; \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-shifts}%
\label{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-core-from-vector-line}%
\label{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-line}%
Work in the setting of
Definitions~\ref{def:ordered-e1-factorization}
and~\ref{def:spectral-quantum-group}. Let
\(J_q^{\mathrm{mult}}\colon
\operatorname{Fact}_{\Eone}^{\mathrm{fd}}(U_q(\mathfrak{sl}_M))^{\mathrm{op}}
\longrightarrow
\Factord(\bC^\times;\QGspec(R_{\cA}))\)
be an exact braided-monoidal functor, and write
\(\rho_a\colon \bC^\times\xrightarrow{\sim}\bC^\times\),
\(z\mapsto e^a z\), for the multiplicative dilations.
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\alph*)}]
\item\emph{Intrinsic loop rotation.}
 Assume the spectral compact core \(\mathcal{C}_q^\omega\) is
 realized as a full stable idempotent-complete braided-monoidal
 subcategory of
 \(\Factord(\bC^\times;\QGspec(R_{\cA}))\) closed under
 \(\rho_a^*\). Then
 \(\mathsf T_a^\omega:=\rho_a^*\colon
 \mathcal C_q^\omega\xrightarrow{\sim}\mathcal C_q^\omega\)
 is an exact braided-monoidal autoequivalence for every
 \(a\in\mathbb C\), with
 \(\mathsf T_{a+b}^\omega\cong
 \mathsf T_a^\omega\circ \mathsf T_b^\omega\) and
 \(\mathsf T_0^\omega\cong \id\).

\item\emph{Core from vector line.}
 Assume \(J_q^{\mathrm{mult}}\) restricts to an equivalence
 \(\mathcal L_q^{\mathrm{vec,fd}}
 \xrightarrow{\sim}
 \mathcal L_q^{\mathrm{vec,mult}}\)
 and each \(\rho_a^*\) preserves
 \(\mathcal L_q^{\mathrm{vec,mult}}\). Let
 \(\mathcal C_{q,\mathrm{mult}}^\omega\) be the smallest full stable
 idempotent-complete braided-monoidal subcategory containing
 \(\mathcal L_q^{\mathrm{vec,mult}}\). Then every \(\rho_a^*\)
 restricts to
 \(\mathcal C_{q,\mathrm{mult}}^\omega\xrightarrow{\sim}
 \mathcal C_{q,\mathrm{mult}}^\omega\),
 \(J_q^{\mathrm{mult}}\) is an exact braided-monoidal equivalence
 \(\operatorname{Fact}_{\Eone}^{\mathrm{fd}}(U_q(\mathfrak{sl}_M))^{\mathrm{op}}
 \xrightarrow{\sim}
 \mathcal C_{q,\mathrm{mult}}^\omega\),
 and \(\mathcal C_{q,\mathrm{mult}}^\omega\) is a multiplicative
 spectral realization of the spectral compact core.

\item\emph{Seed-line forcing.}
 Fix $V(0)\in \mathcal L_q^{\mathrm{vec,fd}}$ and one ambient
 object
 $V^{\mathrm{mult}}(0)\in
 \Factord(\bC^\times;\allowbreak\QGspec(R_{\cA}))$;
 set
 $V^{\mathrm{mult}}(a):=\rho_a^*V^{\mathrm{mult}}(0)$.
 If $J_q^{\mathrm{mult}}$ restricts to an equivalence on the
 one-object subcategory generated by~$V(0)$ and intertwines
 $\mathsf T_a^{\mathrm{fd}}$ with~$\rho_a^*$ on the source
 vector line, then
 $\mathcal L_q^{\mathrm{vec,fd}}
 \xrightarrow{\sim}
 \mathcal L_q^{\mathrm{vec,mult}}$.
\end{enumerate}
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
\textup{(a)}
Each \(\rho_a\) is an automorphism of \(\bC^\times\), so \(\rho_a^*\)
is an exact braided-monoidal autoequivalence of the ambient category.
The closure hypothesis restricts it to \(\mathcal C_q^\omega\), and
\(\rho_{a+b}=\rho_a\circ\rho_b\) gives the group law.

\textup{(b)}
\(\rho_a^*\) preserves the generating line by hypothesis, hence the
thick closure. The source is the thick closure of its vector line
(Lemmas~\ref{lem:quantum-fd-vector-fundamental-generation}
and~\ref{lem:quantum-fd-fundamental-generation}); since
\(J_q^{\mathrm{mult}}\) is exact braided monoidal and an equivalence
on that line, the thick-closure argument of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-realization-formal}
upgrades it.

\textup{(c)}
The intertwining forces
\(J_q^{\mathrm{mult}}(V(a))\cong V^{\mathrm{mult}}(a)\), giving
essential surjectivity. Shifts reduce every Hom pair to
\((V(0),V(b-a))\), and the seed equivalence gives full faithfulness.
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[One-seed closure: four variants;
\ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-seed-realization}%
\label{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-one-seed}%
\label{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-vector-line}%
\label{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-ambient-vector-line}%
Each of the following hypotheses forces the full spectral DK-5 packet:
completed vector line, ordered vector packet, completed fundamental
packet, ordered tensor-generator packet, spectral compact core, and
ambient spectral category are all formal.
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\alph*)}]
\item\emph{Seed-and-shift datum.}
 Work in the setting of
 Propositions~\ref{prop:quantum-fd-vector-seed-shifts}
 and~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-realization-formal}. Let
 \(J_q^\omega\) be an exact braided monoidal functor to
 \(\mathcal{C}_q^\omega\). Assume there is a completed vector seed
 \(V^\omega(0)\in \mathcal{C}_q^\omega\), an exact braided-monoidal
 shift family \(\mathsf{T}_a^\omega\) with
 \(\mathsf{T}_{a+b}^\omega\cong
 \mathsf{T}_a^\omega\circ \mathsf{T}_b^\omega\) and
 \(\mathsf{T}_0^\omega\cong \id\), and that setting
 \(V^\omega(a):=\mathsf{T}_a^\omega(V^\omega(0))\), the functor
 \(J_q^\omega\) identifies \(V(0)\) with \(V^\omega(0)\) and
 intertwines source and target shifts. Then \(J_q^\omega\) restricts
 to an equivalence on the vector line and extends to the full compact
 core and its ind-completion.

\item\emph{One multiplicative seed.}
 Work in the setting of~\textup{(a)} and
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-shifts}.
 If there is a completed vector seed
 \(V^\omega(0)\in \mathcal C_q^\omega\) with
 \(J_q^\omega(V(0))\cong V^\omega(0)\), and \(J_q^\omega\)
 intertwines source shifts with the target pullback family
 \(\mathsf T_a^\omega=\rho_a^*\), then the hypotheses
 of~\textup{(a)} are automatic.

\item\emph{Vector-line realization.}
 Work in the setting of
 Propositions~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-vector-line}
 and~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-shifts}.
 If \(J_q^\omega\) restricts to an equivalence
 \(\mathcal L_q^{\mathrm{vec,fd}}
 \xrightarrow{\sim}
 \mathcal L_q^{\mathrm{vec}}\),
 then the hypotheses of~\textup{(a)} are automatic.

\item\emph{Ambient vector-line realization.}
 Assume the hypotheses of
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-core-from-vector-line},
 and let \(\mathcal C_{q,\mathrm{mult}}^\omega\) be the resulting
 multiplicative spectral compact core. Then \(J_q^{\mathrm{mult}}\)
 restricts to an equivalence on the source vector line, and the
 ordered vector packet, completed fundamental packet, ordered
 tensor-generator packet, compact core, and ambient completed spectral
 category
 \(\operatorname{Rep}^{\mathrm{spec}}(\QGspec(R_{\cA}))^{\mathrm{op}}
 \simeq
 \operatorname{Ind}(\mathcal C_{q,\mathrm{mult}}^\omega)\)
 are all formal from that ambient vector-line realization.
\end{enumerate}
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
\textup{(a)}
The shifts preserve \(\mathcal{L}^{\mathrm{vec}}_{q}\), so
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-vector-seed} forces the
vector-line equivalence.
Propositions~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-vector-line},
\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-vector-packet},
\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-fundamental-packet}, and
\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-realization-formal}
promote it through the ordered vector packet,
fundamental packet, generator packet, and full compact core.
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-packet-ind} gives the
ind-completion.

\textup{(b)}
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-shifts}
constructs \(\mathsf T_a^\omega=\rho_a^*\) intrinsically; setting
\(V^\omega(a):=\mathsf T_a^\omega(V^\omega(0))\) recovers the
hypotheses of~\textup{(a)}.

\textup{(c)}
Propositions~\ref{prop:quantum-fd-vector-seed-shifts}
and~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-seed-shift-construction} construct
and transport the seed-and-shift datum;
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-core-shifts} extends it to
the compact core. On the multiplicative locus, the target shifts are
intrinsic by
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-shifts}.

\textup{(d)}
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-core-from-vector-line}
constructs the compact core;~\textup{(c)} gives the sub-packet
formality; Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-packet-ind} gives
the ambient ind-completion.
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[Schur-simple ambient seed criterion for the
multiplicative spectral vector line; \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-schur-seed-line}
Work in the setting of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-line}.
Assume that:
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\roman*)}]
\item there is an isomorphism
 \[
 J_q^{\mathrm{mult}}(V(0))\cong V^{\mathrm{mult}}(0);
 \]
\item the ambient seed is Schur-simple:
 \[
 \End(V^{\mathrm{mult}}(0))\cong \mathbb C;
 \]
\item on the source vector line,
 \(J_q^{\mathrm{mult}}\) intertwines the standard source loop-rotation
 autoequivalences \(\mathsf T_a^{\mathrm{fd}}\) with the ambient
 dilation pullbacks \(\rho_a^*\).
\end{enumerate}
Then the hypotheses of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-line}
are automatic. Consequently the restriction of \(J_q^{\mathrm{mult}}\)
to the source vector line is an exact braided-monoidal equivalence
\[
\mathcal L_q^{\mathrm{vec,fd}}
\xrightarrow{\sim}
\mathcal L_q^{\mathrm{vec,mult}}.
\]

\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Schur simplicity on both sides
(Lemma~\ref{lem:quantum-fd-vector-seed-schur} and
assumption~\textup{(ii)}) makes the one-object subcategories
equivalent after choosing~\textup{(i)}. Apply
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-line}.
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[One ambient multiplicative vector seed closes the
spectral DK-5 side; \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-ambient-one-seed}
Assume the hypotheses of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-line}.
Let
\[
\mathcal C_{q,\mathrm{mult}}^\omega
\subset
\Factord(\bC^\times;\QGspec(R_{\cA}))
\]
be the smallest full stable idempotent-complete braided-monoidal
subcategory containing the ambient dilation orbit
\(\mathcal L_q^{\mathrm{vec,mult}}\) of \(V^{\mathrm{mult}}(0)\).
Then:
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\alph*)}]
\item \(\mathcal C_{q,\mathrm{mult}}^\omega\) is exactly the
 multiplicative spectral compact core forced by that single ambient
 vector seed;
\item the completed vector line, ordered vector packet, completed
 fundamental packet, ordered tensor-generator packet, compact core,
 and ambient completed spectral category are all formal from that
 seed.
\end{enumerate}

\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Apply
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-line}
to verify the hypotheses of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-core-from-vector-line},
then
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-ambient-vector-line}.
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[One Schur-simple ambient multiplicative vector seed
closes the spectral DK-5 side; \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-ambient-schur-seed}
Work in the setting of
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-schur-seed-line}.
Let
\[
\mathcal C_{q,\mathrm{mult}}^\omega
\subset
\Factord(\bC^\times;\QGspec(R_{\cA}))
\]
be the smallest full stable idempotent-complete braided-monoidal
subcategory containing the ambient dilation orbit
\(\mathcal L_q^{\mathrm{vec,mult}}\) of \(V^{\mathrm{mult}}(0)\).
Then the completed vector line, ordered vector packet, completed
fundamental packet, ordered tensor-generator packet, compact core, and
ambient completed spectral category are all formal from that single
Schur-simple ambient vector seed.

\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-schur-seed-line}
supplies the hypotheses of
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-ambient-one-seed}.
\end{proof}

\begin{theorem}[Spectral DK-5 seed-pair reduction hierarchy;
\ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-mono}%
\label{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-mono}%
\label{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-trig}%
\label{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-trig}%
\label{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-channels}%
\label{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-single-line}%
\label{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-exchange}%
\label{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-exchange-mult}%
\label{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-alt-mult}%
Work in the setting of
Definitions~\ref{def:ordered-e1-factorization}
and~\ref{def:spectral-quantum-group}. Fix one ambient object
\(V^{\mathrm{mult}}(0)\in \Factord(\bC^\times;\QGspec(R_{\cA}))\)
and define its dilation orbit by
\(V^{\mathrm{mult}}(a):=\rho_a^*V^{\mathrm{mult}}(0)\).
For \(a,b\in\mathbb C\), write
\(\mathsf B_{a,b}^{\mathrm{mult}}\) for the ambient two-point braid
monodromy operator and \(\mathsf B_{a,b}^{\mathrm{fd}}\) for the
source two-point trigonometric braid operator on the standard
quantum-loop vector line. Then the following successive reductions
hold.
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\alph*)}]
\item\emph{Monodromy from seed pair.}
 After the canonical identification
 \(V^{\mathrm{mult}}(a)\boxtimes V^{\mathrm{mult}}(b)
 \cong \rho_a^*(V^{\mathrm{mult}}(0)\boxtimes V^{\mathrm{mult}}(b-a))\),
 one has
 \(\mathsf B_{a,b}^{\mathrm{mult}}
 \cong \rho_a^*(\mathsf B_{0,b-a}^{\mathrm{mult}})\).
 On every ordered tensor product, the full braid-group action is
 generated by the one-parameter family
 \(\{\mathsf B_{0,c}^{\mathrm{mult}}\}_{c\in\mathbb C}\) via
 dilation pullbacks. After the Schur-simple ambient seed, the only
 remaining local geometric datum is that seed-pair monodromy family.

\item\emph{Trigonometric identity.}
 The braid-group action on the ambient vector packet agrees with the
 standard source trigonometric action if and only if
 \(\mathsf B_{0,c}^{\mathrm{mult}} \cong
 \mathsf B_{0,c}^{\mathrm{fd}}\) for every \(c\in\mathbb C\).

\item\emph{Channel decomposition.}
 Assume further that for every \(c\), both
 \(\mathsf B_{0,c}^{\mathrm{fd}}\) and
 \(\mathsf B_{0,c}^{\mathrm{mult}}\) intertwine the diagonal
 \(\mathfrak{sl}_M\)-action on \(V\otimes V\). Then the
 trigonometric seed-pair identity holds if and only if the two
 operators act by the same scalar on \(\operatorname{Sym}^2(V)\) and
 on \(\Lambda^2(V)\); equivalently, it is enough to check on
 \(e_1\otimes e_1\) and \(e_1\otimes e_2-e_2\otimes e_1\).

\item\emph{Mixed-tensor reduction.}
 Assume \(M\ge 2\) and that for every \(c\) the source and ambient
 operators agree on the highest-weight line
 (\(\mathsf B_{0,c}^{\mathrm{mult}}(e_1\otimes e_1)
 = \mathsf B_{0,c}^{\mathrm{fd}}(e_1\otimes e_1)\)).
 Then the trigonometric identity holds if and only if the single
 mixed-tensor identity
 \(\mathsf B_{0,c}^{\mathrm{mult}}(e_1\otimes e_2)
 = \mathsf B_{0,c}^{\mathrm{fd}}(e_1\otimes e_2)\) holds.

\item\emph{Exchange coefficient.}
 Under the hypotheses of~\textup{(d)}, write
 \(\mathsf B_{0,c}^{\bullet}(e_1\otimes e_2)
 = \alpha^{\bullet}(c)\,e_1\otimes e_2
 + \beta^{\bullet}(c)\,e_2\otimes e_1\)
 for \(\bullet\in\{\mathrm{fd},\mathrm{mult}\}\).
 Then the trigonometric identity is equivalent to the single scalar
 identity \(\beta^{\mathrm{mult}}(c)=\beta^{\mathrm{fd}}(c)\).
 Both families are \(2\pi i\)-periodic, hence descend to functions
 \(\beta_\times^{\mathrm{fd}},\beta_\times^{\mathrm{mult}}\) of the
 multiplicative ratio \(e^c\), and the identity becomes
 \(\beta_\times^{\mathrm{mult}}=\beta_\times^{\mathrm{fd}}\).

\item\emph{Antisymmetric-channel character.}
 Under the hypotheses of~\textup{(e)}, there exist unique scalar
 functions
 \(\lambda_{\mathrm{alt},\times}^{\mathrm{fd}},
 \lambda_{\mathrm{alt},\times}^{\mathrm{mult}}\) of the
 multiplicative spectral ratio such that
 \(\mathsf B_{0,c}^{\bullet}(e_1\otimes e_2-e_2\otimes e_1)
 = \lambda_{\mathrm{alt},\times}^{\bullet}(e^c)
 (e_1\otimes e_2-e_2\otimes e_1)\).
 The trigonometric seed-pair identity is equivalent to
 \(\lambda_{\mathrm{alt},\times}^{\mathrm{mult}}
 = \lambda_{\mathrm{alt},\times}^{\mathrm{fd}}\).
\end{enumerate}
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
\textup{(a)}
Functoriality of \(\rho_a^*\) transports
\(\mathsf B_{0,b-a}^{\mathrm{mult}}\) to
\(\mathsf B_{a,b}^{\mathrm{mult}}\).
\(B_n\) is generated by adjacent transpositions, and each adjacent
operator is obtained from the seed-pair family by dilation pullback.
The Schur-simple reduction follows from
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-ambient-schur-seed}.

\textup{(b)}
The source braid-group action is generated by
\(\{\mathsf B_{0,c}^{\mathrm{fd}}\}\) via the same dilation argument
(using \(\mathsf T_a^{\mathrm{fd}}\) in place of \(\rho_a^*\)).
Since both sides are generated by their respective seed-pair families,
the full actions agree if and only if the seed-pair families agree.

\textup{(c)}
Diagonal \(\mathfrak{sl}_M\)-equivariance forces both operators to
preserve
\(V\otimes V\cong \operatorname{Sym}^2(V)\oplus \Lambda^2(V)\).
Schur's lemma reduces the comparison to two channel scalars, detected
by the highest-weight generators.

\textup{(d)}
The highest-weight normalization forces
\(\lambda_{\mathrm{sym}}^{\mathrm{mult}}(c)=
\lambda_{\mathrm{sym}}^{\mathrm{fd}}(c)\).
Writing \(e_1\otimes e_2=\frac12(s+a)\) with
\(s\in\operatorname{Sym}^2(V)\), \(a\in\Lambda^2(V)\), the
mixed-tensor identity and linear independence of \(e_1\otimes e_2\)
and \(e_2\otimes e_1\) force the antisymmetric channel scalar to
agree as well, giving~\textup{(c)}.

\textup{(e)}
Under the common symmetric channel scalar, the exchange coefficient
satisfies
\(\beta(c)=(\lambda_{\mathrm{sym}}(c)-\lambda_{\mathrm{alt}}(c))/2\),
so \(\beta^{\mathrm{mult}}=\beta^{\mathrm{fd}}\) is equivalent to
equality of channel scalars and hence of full mixed-tensor outputs.
Both families are \(2\pi i\)-periodic (\(V(c+2\pi i)\cong V(c)\) on
the source, \(\rho_{c+2\pi i}=\rho_c\) on the ambient side), hence
descend to the multiplicative ratio.

\textup{(f)}
The antisymmetric channel scalars are likewise \(2\pi i\)-periodic,
hence descend to multiplicative-ratio functions. Under highest-weight
normalization, equality of exchange coefficients is equivalent to
equality of these antisymmetric-channel characters.
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[On the realized spectral packet locus, the ambient
spectral category is the ind-completion of the spectral compact core;
\ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-packet-ind}
Assume the hypotheses of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-realization-formal}. On
this realized packet locus, define the ambient completed spectral
category by
\[
\operatorname{Rep}^{\mathrm{spec}}(\QGspec(R_{\cA}))^{\mathrm{op}}
:=
\operatorname{Ind}(\mathcal{C}_q^\omega).
\]
Then
\(\operatorname{Rep}^{\mathrm{spec}}(\QGspec(R_{\cA}))^{\mathrm{op}}\)
is presentable, stable, and compactly generated, and its compact
objects are exactly \(\mathcal{C}_q^\omega\). Equivalently, there is a
canonical exact colimit-preserving equivalence
\[
\operatorname{Rep}^{\mathrm{spec}}(\QGspec(R_{\cA}))^{\mathrm{op}}
\xrightarrow{\sim}
\operatorname{Ind}(\mathcal{C}_q^\omega).
\]
In particular, the ambient completed spectral category is compactly
generated by the completed fundamental spectral packet
\(\mathcal{G}^{\mathrm{fund}}_{q}\).
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
This is the standard ind-completion package for a small stable
idempotent-complete category: by definition
\(\operatorname{Rep}^{\mathrm{spec}}(\QGspec(R_{\cA}))^{\mathrm{op}}
= \operatorname{Ind}(\mathcal{C}_q^\omega)\), and the resulting
category is presentable, stable, and compactly generated with compact
objects exactly \(\mathcal{C}_q^\omega\) by the standard universal
properties of ind-completion for small stable idempotent-complete
categories \textup{(}Lurie, \emph{HTT}, \S5.3.5, \S5.5.7\textup{)}.
\end{proof}

\begin{proposition}[Canonical completed dg fundamental packet from the
theorematic finite RTT quotients; \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{prop:yangian-dg-fundamental-packet-realization}
Assume the data and hypotheses \textup{(i)}--\textup{(vii)} of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion}. Let
\[
\mathcal{G}^{\mathrm{fund,fd}}_{Y}
\subset
\operatorname{Fact}_{\Eone}^{\mathrm{fd}}(Y_\hbar(\mathfrak{sl}_M))
\]
be the full subcategory generated by finite ordered tensor products of
fundamental evaluation objects. For
\(M\in\mathcal{G}^{\mathrm{fund,fd}}_{Y}\), let \(M_{\le N}\) be its
standard finite-stage evaluation image over \(Y_{\le N}\) under the
compatible quotient comparison of
assumption~\textup{(vi)}. Then the tower \(\{M_{\le N}\}_N\) defines a
continuous completed dg module
\[
J_{Y,\mathrm{pkt}}^\omega(M)
:=
\varprojlim_N M_{\le N}
\]
over \(\Ydg_{\cA}\), and these assignments assemble into a canonical
exact braided monoidal functor
\[
J_{Y,\mathrm{pkt}}^\omega\colon
\mathcal{G}^{\mathrm{fund,fd}}_{Y}
\longrightarrow
\operatorname{Mod}^{\mathrm{comp}}(\Ydg_{\cA}).
\]
Let \(\mathcal{G}^{\mathrm{fund}}_{Y}\) denote its essential image.
Then \(J_{Y,\mathrm{pkt}}^\omega\) is an exact braided monoidal
equivalence
\[
\mathcal{G}^{\mathrm{fund,fd}}_{Y}
\xrightarrow{\sim}
\mathcal{G}^{\mathrm{fund}}_{Y}.
\]

\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
Assumption~\textup{(vi)} identifies each finite quotient with
\(Y_{\le N}\) compatibly with evaluation modules. The inverse limit
\(\varprojlim_N M_{\le N}\) is then a continuous module over
\(\Ydg_{\cA}\) by assumption~\textup{(v)}. Exactness and braided
monoidality are checked stagewise using
assumptions~\textup{(i)}--\textup{(iv)} and~\textup{(vi)}.
\end{proof}

\begin{proposition}[Canonical exact braided-monoidal extension of the
dg packet; \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{prop:yangian-dk5-dg-extension-existence}
Assume the hypotheses of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dg-fundamental-packet-realization}. Let
\[
\mathcal{C}_Y^\omega
:=
\operatorname{thick}^{\mathrm{idemp}}
\bigl(\mathcal{G}^{\mathrm{fund}}_{Y}\bigr)
\subset
\operatorname{Mod}^{\mathrm{comp}}(\Ydg_{\cA}).
\]
Then the packet functor \(J_{Y,\mathrm{pkt}}^\omega\) extends to an
exact braided monoidal functor
\[
J_Y^\omega\colon
\operatorname{Fact}_{\Eone}^{\mathrm{fd}}(Y_\hbar(\mathfrak{sl}_M))
\longrightarrow
\mathcal{C}_Y^\omega
\]
whose restriction to \(\mathcal{G}^{\mathrm{fund,fd}}_{Y}\) is
\(J_{Y,\mathrm{pkt}}^\omega\). This extension is unique up to unique
natural isomorphism.

\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
The stable idempotent-complete braided monoidal target
\(\mathcal{C}_Y^\omega\) allows unique thick-closure extension of
\(J_{Y,\mathrm{pkt}}^\omega\) from
\(\mathcal{G}^{\mathrm{fund,fd}}_{Y}\) to the full source
(Lemma~\ref{lem:yangian-fd-fundamental-generation}). Uniqueness
follows as in
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk3-generated-core}.
\end{proof}

\begin{proposition}[dg compact-core realization is formal from
extension of the completed fundamental packet;
\ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{prop:yangian-dk5-dg-realization-formal}
Assume the hypotheses of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-dg-extension-existence}. Let
\[
\mathcal{C}_Y^\omega
:=
\operatorname{thick}^{\mathrm{idemp}}
\bigl(\mathcal{G}^{\mathrm{fund}}_{Y}\bigr)
\subset
\operatorname{Mod}^{\mathrm{comp}}(\Ydg_{\cA}).
\]
Then \(J_Y^\omega\) is an exact braided monoidal equivalence.

\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
Since \(J_Y^\omega\) is exact braided monoidal and an equivalence on
\(\mathcal{G}^{\mathrm{fund,fd}}_{Y}\), the thick-closure argument of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-realization-formal} upgrades
it to an equivalence on the full closures
(Lemma~\ref{lem:yangian-fd-fundamental-generation}).
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[Compact generation of the completed dg module
category identifies the ambient dg side with the ind-completion of the
dg compact core;
\ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-dk5-dg-packet-ind}
Assume the hypotheses of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-dg-realization-formal}. On this
realized packet locus, define the ambient completed dg module category
by
\[
\operatorname{Mod}^{\mathrm{comp}}(\Ydg_{\cA})
:=
\operatorname{Ind}(\mathcal{C}_Y^\omega).
\]
Then \(\operatorname{Mod}^{\mathrm{comp}}(\Ydg_{\cA})\) is presentable,
stable, and compactly generated, and its compact objects are exactly
\(\mathcal{C}_Y^\omega\). Equivalently, there is a canonical exact
colimit-preserving equivalence
\[
\operatorname{Mod}^{\mathrm{comp}}(\Ydg_{\cA})
\xrightarrow{\sim}
\operatorname{Ind}(\mathcal{C}_Y^\omega).
\]
In particular, \(\operatorname{Mod}^{\mathrm{comp}}(\Ydg_{\cA})\) is
compactly generated by the completed fundamental dg-shifted packet
\(\mathcal{G}^{\mathrm{fund}}_{Y}\).

\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
This is again the standard ind-completion package for a small stable
idempotent-complete category: by definition
\(\operatorname{Mod}^{\mathrm{comp}}(\Ydg_{\cA})
= \operatorname{Ind}(\mathcal{C}_Y^\omega)\), and the resulting
category is presentable, stable, and compactly generated with compact
objects exactly \(\mathcal{C}_Y^\omega\) by the standard universal
properties of ind-completion for small stable idempotent-complete
categories \textup{(}Lurie, \emph{HTT}, \S5.3.5, \S5.5.7\textup{)}.
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[Given dg compact-core realization, the remaining
DK-5 input is spectral vector seed-and-shift realization;
\ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-dk5-dg-half-only}
Assume the hypotheses of
Corollary~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-dg-local-closure}. Assume further
that:
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\roman*)}]
\item the completed dg-shifted and spectral categories are presentable,
 stable, and compactly generated, with compact objects exactly
 \(\mathcal{C}_Y^\omega\) and \(\mathcal{C}_q^\omega\);
\item the spectral compact core admits an exact braided monoidal
 functor \(J_q^\omega\) whose restriction to the vector evaluation
 line is an equivalence onto the completed vector spectral line, as in
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-vector-line}; and
\item there exists an exact braided monoidal equivalence
 \[
 J_Y^\omega\colon
 \operatorname{Fact}_{\Eone}^{\mathrm{fd}}(Y_\hbar(\mathfrak{sl}_M))
 \xrightarrow{\sim}
 \mathcal{C}_Y^\omega
 \]
 identifying the fundamental evaluation objects with the completed
 fundamental dg-shifted packet.
\end{enumerate}
Then the standard type-$A$ Yangian DK-5 packet closes.

\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Propositions~\ref{prop:quantum-fd-vector-seed-shifts},
\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-seed-shift-construction},
and~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-core-shifts} transport the standard
seed-and-shift datum to the spectral compact core.
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-seed-realization} closes the
spectral packet. Together with the dg hypotheses,
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-core-realization} closes DK-5.
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[DK-5 closes once the compact cores realize a
finite-dimensional factorization DK pair; \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-dk5-core-realization}
Assume the hypotheses of
Corollary~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-dg-local-closure}. Assume further
that:
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\roman*)}]
\item the completed dg-shifted and spectral categories are presentable,
 stable, and compactly generated, with compact objects exactly
 $\mathcal{C}_Y^\omega$ and $\mathcal{C}_q^\omega$;
\item the compact cores are exact braided monoidal realizations of the
 chosen finite-dimensional factorization DK pair in the sense of
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-core-realization}.
\end{enumerate}
Then the standard type-$A$ Yangian DK-5 packet closes.

\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Apply Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-core-realization} for the
compact-core equivalence, then
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-ind-extension} for the ambient
extension.
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[Type-\texorpdfstring{$A$}{A} MC4 reduction chain:
 five closure criteria; \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-typea-mc4-closure-criterion}%
\label{cor:yangian-typea-degree2-plus-generators}%
\label{cor:yangian-typea-casimir-plus-generators}%
\label{cor:yangian-typea-factorization-local-closure}%
\label{cor:yangian-typea-shared-seed-plus-generators}%
Assume the hypotheses of
Propositions~\ref{prop:yangian-dk4-typea-frontier}
and~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-compact-generators}.
The standard type-$A$ Yangian MC4 packet admits the following
successive reductions.
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\roman*)}]
\item\emph{Minimal closure.}
 MC4 closes once the dg-shifted or factorization one-factor kernel is
 identified with the standard normalized RTT residue on the
 fundamental evaluation line (under the symmetry and normalization
 hypotheses of
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk4-typea-frontier} this is equivalent
 to
 \(
 \Xi_a(e_1\otimes e_2)=-\hbar(e_2\otimes e_1)
 \)), and the compact-generator comparison
 $\mathcal{G}^{\mathrm{fund}}_Y \to \mathcal{G}^{\mathrm{fund}}_q$
 is an equivalence.

\item\emph{One-loop exactness.}
 Assume further the one-loop exactness and seed-normalization
 hypotheses of
 Proposition~\ref{prop:dg-shifted-rtt-degree2-mixed-tensor-criterion}
 and
 Corollary~\ref{prop:dg-shifted-rtt-seed-normalized-coefficient} on
 the standard type-$A$ fundamental line. Then the remaining MC4
 input is the single degree-$2$ coefficient identity
 \[
 r_a^{\mathrm{fund}}(z)(e_1\otimes e_2)
 =
 -\hbar(e_2\otimes e_1),
 \]
 where $r_a^{\mathrm{fund}}(z)$ is induced by
 $r(z)=\tau|_{\deg 2}$ on the ordered fundamental line, together
 with the compact-generator comparison.

\item\emph{Casimir insertion.}
 If in addition the ordered fundamental-line degree-$2$ coefficient is
 the standard trace-zero Casimir insertion
 \[
 r_a^{\mathrm{fund}}(z)\big|_{z_1=z_2}
 =
 -\hbar\,\Omega_{\mathfrak{sl}_M}^{\mathrm{fund}}
 =
 -\hbar\Bigl(P-\frac{1}{M}\id\Bigr),
 \]
 then the local coefficient identity~\textup{(ii)} is automatic, and
 the remaining MC4 input is compact generation plus transport on the
 completed fundamental evaluation packet.

\item\emph{Factorization closure.}
 On the ordered factorization target,
 Corollary~\ref{prop:factorization-fundamental-casimir-identity}
 supplies the Casimir hypothesis of~\textup{(iii)} automatically.
 Hence the remaining MC4 input on the factorization side is compact
 generation plus fundamental-packet transport.

\item\emph{Shared seed closure.}
 Assume the hypotheses of~\textup{(iv)} on the ordered factorization
 target and of
 Corollary~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-dg-local-closure} on an ordered
 dg-shifted target presented by the same ordered bar seed. Then the
 local MC4 packet is automatic on both sides, and the remaining
 standard type-$A$ Yangian MC4 input is exactly the compact-generator
 comparison
 \[
 \mathcal{G}^{\mathrm{fund}}_Y
 \xrightarrow{\sim}
 \mathcal{G}^{\mathrm{fund}}_q.
 \]
\end{enumerate}
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
\textup{(i)}
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk4-typea-frontier} reduces DK-4 to the
mixed-tensor coefficient;
Proposition~\ref{prop:dg-shifted-rtt-degree2-fundamental-casimir}
and Corollary~\ref{prop:factorization-fundamental-casimir-identity}
show the Casimir insertion forces it.
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-compact-generators} reduces DK-5 to
compact generators.

\textup{(ii)}
Corollary~\ref{prop:dg-shifted-rtt-seed-normalized-coefficient}
identifies the residue with the degree-$2$ coefficient. Under
one-loop exactness
(Proposition~\ref{prop:dg-shifted-rtt-degree2-mixed-tensor-criterion}),
this forces the DK-4 content of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk4-typea-frontier}. The remaining
DK-5 input is
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-fundamental-packet}.

\textup{(iii)}
Proposition~\ref{prop:dg-shifted-rtt-degree2-fundamental-casimir}
forces \(\beta_a=-1\), which gives the coefficient
identity~\textup{(ii)}.

\textup{(iv)}
Corollary~\ref{prop:factorization-fundamental-casimir-identity}
supplies the Casimir hypothesis of~\textup{(iii)}.

\textup{(v)}
Part~\textup{(iv)} closes the factorization side;
Corollary~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-dg-local-closure} transports via
the shared seed.
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-compact-generators} reduces the
remaining DK-5 packet to compact generators.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}[Exact extra input for DK-5]
\label{rem:yangian-dk5-input}
After Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk4-typea-frontier}, the remaining
DK-5 packet is the compact-core categorical packet:
\textup{(i)}~on the dg side,
Propositions~\ref{prop:yangian-dg-fundamental-packet-realization},
\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-dg-extension-existence},
and~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-dg-realization-formal} construct and extend
the canonical dg packet, and
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-dg-packet-ind} removes the remaining
dg obstruction;
\textup{(ii)}~on the spectral side, realize the standard vector
seed-and-shift datum
(Propositions~\ref{prop:quantum-fd-vector-seed-shifts},
\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-seed-shift-construction},
\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-core-shifts}); on the multiplicative
locus this contracts to one Schur-simple ambient vector seed
(Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-ambient-schur-seed})
and then to one antisymmetric-channel character
(Proposition~\ref{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-alt-mult});
\textup{(iii)}~with both compact-core realizations,
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-core-realization} closes DK-5 via
ind-extension (Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-ind-extension}).
\end{remark}

\begin{remark}[MC4 boundary for Yangian towers]
\label{rem:yangian-mc4-boundary}
The finite RTT Yangians are theorematic (bar-cobar, $R\mapsto R^{-1}$,
evaluation-locus DK square). The genuine MC4 input is
Hypothesis~\textup{(ii)} of Conjecture~\ref{conj:full-dk-bridge}: the
RTT-adapted realization of the canonical H-level target
(Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-canonical-hlevel-target}).
The standard RTT tower supplies the completed M-level package
(Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-standard-mc4-package}), and
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-hlevel-comparison-criterion} makes the
comparison formal once one supplies an RTT-adapted dg realization whose
finite RTT quotients recover the theorematic stages and whose completed
bar/cobar comparison data is compatible with the standard RTT tower.
For standard type-$A$,
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk4-typea-frontier} sharpens DK-4 to
one mixed-tensor residue check, while the remaining DK-5 work is the
compact-core realization and extension packet recorded in
Remark~\ref{rem:yangian-dk5-input}. On the spectral side, the
reduction chain contracts the live input to one antisymmetric-channel
character on the multiplicative spectral line
(Proposition~\ref{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-alt-mult}).
MC5 begins only after this H-level comparison packet is in place.
\end{remark}

\begin{remark}[What the Yangian tower still has to prove]
\label{rem:yangian-mc4-checklist}
By Proposition~\ref{prop:mc4-reduction-principle}, the Yangian-tower
completion programme, now resolved by the strong completion-tower theorem (Theorem~\ref{thm:completed-bar-cobar-strong}), originally broke into four checks:
\textup{(1)}~finite RTT truncations in the proved $\Eone$-Koszul regime;
\textup{(2)}~compatible descent of finite-stage bar/cobar
(Proposition~\ref{prop:inverse-limit-differential-continuity});
\textup{(3)}~Mittag--Leffler on
$\{H^m(\bar B(Y_{\le N}))\}_N$
(Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-weight-cutoff});
\textup{(4)}~inverse-limit identification
(Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-rtt-completion-identification}).
Items~\textup{(1)}--\textup{(3)} are absorbed by the strong
completion-tower theorem: the finite RTT stages lie in
$\CompCl(\Fft)$, the coefficient-stability criterion
(Theorem~\ref{thm:coefficient-stability-criterion}) gives automatic
Mittag--Leffler, and the reduced-weight windows
(Theorem~\ref{thm:window-locality}) make each finite check
explicit. The Yangian jet principle
\ifannalsedition\else
(Conjecture~\ref{conj:jet-principle})
\fi predicts that reduced-weight-$q$
bar windows determine Yangian jets through order~$z^{-q}$.
For~\textup{(4)},
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-hlevel-comparison-criterion} reduces the
H-level comparison to constructing a filtered model whose finite
quotients match the proved stages; in type~$A$,
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk4-typea-frontier} reduces this to one
residue check, and the dg fundamental packet is already constructed by
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dg-fundamental-packet-realization}.
\end{remark}

\begin{proposition}[Yangian tower criterion from finite RTT stages;
\ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{prop:yangian-tower-mc4-criterion}
Let
\[
Y = \varprojlim_N Y_{\le N}
\]
be a separated complete Yangian tower assembled from finite RTT stages.
Assume:
\begin{enumerate}
\item each $Y_{\le N}$ lies in the proved $\Eone$-Koszul regime of this
 chapter;
\item the transition maps $Y_{\le N+1} \to Y_{\le N}$ are compatible
 with the finite-stage bar complexes and bar-cobar
 quasi-isomorphisms;
\item for every cohomological degree~$m$, the inverse system
 $\{H^m(\bar B(Y_{\le N}))\}_N$ is eventually constant; and
\item the transition maps define an inverse system of curved dg
 coalgebras on the finite-stage bar complexes.
\end{enumerate}
Then the completed Yangian bar object
\[
\widehat{\bar B}(Y) := \varprojlim_N \bar B(Y_{\le N})
\]
is a separated complete pro-nilpotent curved dg coalgebra and the
canonical comparison map
\[
\Omega\bigl(\widehat{\bar B}(Y)\bigr) \xrightarrow{\sim} Y
\]
is a quasi-isomorphism. This gives the M-level completed bar-cobar
package for the Yangian tower under the stated inverse-limit
hypotheses. As in the $\mathcal{W}_\infty$ case, the eventual-constancy
hypothesis may be weakened to eventual surjectivity on finite-dimensional
weight slices by Corollary~\ref{cor:mc4-surjective-criterion}.
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
Assumption~\textup{(iii)} is exactly the stabilization hypothesis of
Corollary~\ref{cor:mc4-degreewise-stabilization}, and
Assumptions~\textup{(i)}, \textup{(ii)}, and~\textup{(iv)} identify the
Yangian tower with the general inverse-limit setting of
Proposition~\ref{prop:mc4-reduction-principle}, while
Proposition~\ref{prop:inverse-limit-differential-continuity} supplies
the continuity of the completed bar and cobar differentials.
Applying Corollary~\ref{cor:mc4-degreewise-stabilization} to the tower
$\{\bar B(Y_{\le N})\}_N$ yields the stated completed bar-cobar
quasi-isomorphism.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}[Standard-tower Yangian frontier]
For the standard type-$A$ RTT tower, the finite-stage M-level package
is theorematic, while the remaining live inputs are the H-level
realization and the post-core DK-5 compact/completed comparison.
Type~$A$ does not close MC3 here:
Theorem~\ref{thm:mc3-type-a-resolution} reduces the old four-package
problem to the remaining compact-completion packet
\textup{(}Conjecture~\ref{conj:dk-compacts-completion}\textup{)}.
Across arbitrary type, the all-types categorical CG/core surface is
already proved \textup{(}Corollary~\ref{cor:mc3-all-types}\textup{)};
what remains is the corresponding post-core extension/completion
packet together with the relevant realization input.
\end{remark}

\begin{corollary}[Standard RTT cutoff for Yangian towers;
\ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-weight-cutoff}
Let $Y_{\le N}$ be the standard RTT truncation retaining the generators
$T_{ij}^{(r)}$ with $r \le N$, and let
$Y = \varprojlim_N Y_{\le N}$ be the resulting inverse-limit tower.
Then the tower of bar complexes $\{\bar B(Y_{\le N})\}_N$ satisfies the
hypotheses of Proposition~\ref{prop:mc4-weight-cutoff} for the total
RTT-level filtration. In particular, for every cohomological degree
$m$ and total RTT level $\ell$, the map
\[
H^m(\bar B(Y_{\le N+1}))_\ell \xrightarrow{\sim}
H^m(\bar B(Y_{\le N}))_\ell
\]
is an isomorphism for all $N \ge \ell$.

Therefore the standard RTT tower already supplies the
surjectivity/stabilization part of MC4. Together with
Proposition~\ref{prop:inverse-limit-differential-continuity} and
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-rtt-completion-identification}, this
reduces the standard RTT tower to the standard-RTT completed M-level
package of Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-standard-mc4-package}.
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
The RTT generators are graded by level~$r$, and the RTT relation is
homogeneous in the total level (Theorem~\ref{thm:yangian-koszul-dual},
Step~2a). A bar chain of total RTT level $\ell$ can therefore involve
only generators $T_{ij}^{(r)}$ with $r \le \ell$. Once $N \ge \ell$,
all such generators already lie in the truncation $Y_{\le N}$, so the
filtered bar subcomplex of levels $\le \ell$ is identical in every
later stage. Proposition~\ref{prop:mc4-weight-cutoff} then gives the
stated stabilization on cohomology slices.
\end{proof}

\begin{proposition}[Inverse-limit identification of the standard RTT
completion; \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{prop:yangian-rtt-completion-identification}
Let $\widehat Y_{\mathrm{RTT}}$ be the coefficientwise RTT completion:
its elements are formal matrices
\[
T(u)=1+\hbar\sum_{r \ge 0} T^{(r)}u^{-r-1}
\]
satisfying the RTT relation coefficientwise, with topology of
coefficientwise convergence in the modes $T_{ij}^{(r)}$. Then the
canonical truncation maps identify this completed RTT algebra with the
standard inverse-limit tower:
\[
\widehat Y_{\mathrm{RTT}} \xrightarrow{\sim} \varprojlim_N Y_{\le N}.
\]
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
For each $N$, truncating the formal matrix after level~$N$ produces
\[
T_{\le N}(u)=1+\hbar\sum_{r=0}^N T^{(r)}u^{-r-1},
\]
which satisfies the finite RTT relations defining $Y_{\le N}$ because
every coefficient of the RTT equation only involves finitely many modes.
This gives compatible algebra maps
$q_N\colon \widehat Y_{\mathrm{RTT}} \to Y_{\le N}$ and hence a map
\[
q\colon \widehat Y_{\mathrm{RTT}} \longrightarrow \varprojlim_N Y_{\le N}.
\]

Conversely, let $(x_N)_N$ be a compatible family in the inverse limit.
Represent $x_N$ by a truncated RTT matrix
$T^{(\le N)}(u)=1+\hbar\sum_{r=0}^N T_N^{(r)}u^{-r-1}$.
Compatibility of the truncation maps implies that for each fixed
$r \ge 0$, the coefficient $T_N^{(r)}$ is independent of $N$ once
$N \ge r$; denote the stable value by $T^{(r)}$. These stable
coefficients assemble into a formal RTT matrix
\[
T(u)=1+\hbar\sum_{r \ge 0} T^{(r)}u^{-r-1}.
\]
To verify the RTT relation coefficientwise, fix a coefficient of
$u^{-a-1}v^{-b-1}$. That coefficient depends only on modes
$T^{(r)}$ with $r \le \max\{a,b\}+1$, so it is already visible in every
finite truncation $Y_{\le N}$ with $N \ge \max\{a,b\}+1$. Since each
$T^{(\le N)}(u)$ satisfies the finite RTT relation, the chosen
coefficient vanishes in the limit. Thus $T(u)$ lies in
$\widehat Y_{\mathrm{RTT}}$.

The constructions are inverse to one another: truncating the recovered
formal RTT matrix returns the original compatible family, and taking the
stable coefficients of a formal RTT matrix recovers it exactly. Hence
$q$ is an isomorphism.
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[Standard RTT tower satisfies the M-level MC4 package;
\ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-standard-mc4-package}
For the standard RTT truncation tower, the completed bar object
\[
\widehat{\bar B}(Y) := \varprojlim_N \bar B(Y_{\le N})
\]
has continuous bar and cobar differentials, and the canonical
comparison map
\[
\Omega\bigl(\widehat{\bar B}(Y)\bigr) \xrightarrow{\sim}
\widehat Y_{\mathrm{RTT}}
\]
is a quasi-isomorphism.
Thus the standard RTT tower supplies the full M-level completed
bar-cobar package for the coefficientwise RTT completion. What remains
open is the H-level comparison of $\widehat Y_{\mathrm{RTT}}$ with the
dg-shifted Yangian or factorization-theoretic completion.
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
The finite RTT stages lie in the proved $\Eone$-Koszul regime, so the
finite-stage bar-cobar quasi-isomorphisms are already available.
Proposition~\ref{prop:inverse-limit-differential-continuity} supplies
continuity of the completed bar and cobar differentials, and
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-weight-cutoff} supplies the
Mittag--Leffler/stabilization input for the standard RTT tower.
Applying Proposition~\ref{prop:mc4-reduction-principle} to that tower
and identifying the target inverse limit by
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-rtt-completion-identification} gives the
stated quasi-isomorphism.
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[H-level comparison criterion for dg-shifted Yangians;
\ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-hlevel-comparison-criterion}
Let $\Ydg_{\cA}$ be a separated complete dg algebra equipped with a
descending RTT-level filtration by closed dg ideals. Assume:
\begin{enumerate}
\item $\Ydg_{\cA}$ is the inverse limit of its finite RTT-level
 quotients;
\item for each $N$ there is a dg algebra quasi-isomorphism
 \[
 \Ydg_{\cA}/F^{N+1}\Ydg_{\cA} \xrightarrow{\sim} Y_{\le N}
 \]
 compatible with the truncation tower; and
\item the quotient tower inherits bar-cobar comparison maps compatible
 with the standard RTT tower and has continuous completed bar and cobar
 differentials.
\end{enumerate}
Then the induced comparison map
\[
\Ydg_{\cA} \xrightarrow{\sim} \widehat Y_{\mathrm{RTT}}
\]
is a quasi-isomorphism, and $\Ydg_{\cA}$ defines the same completed
M-level bar-cobar object as the standard RTT completion. Thus the
remaining Yangian H-level problem is to identify the canonical
formal-moduli target of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-canonical-hlevel-target}, or any chosen
equivalent dg model, with a filtered dg-shifted or factorization model
with theorematic finite RTT quotients. The MC4 structural
framework is proved (Theorem~\ref{thm:completed-bar-cobar-strong});
the finite RTT stages lie in $\CompCl(\Fft)$ and the
coefficient-stability criterion
(Theorem~\ref{thm:coefficient-stability-criterion}) reduces
convergence to window stabilization. Once such an RTT-adapted
realization is supplied, the remaining coefficient
comparison is the exact packet
\[
\mathsf{K}^{\mathrm{line}}_{a,b}(N)
=\mathsf{K}^{\mathrm{RTT}}_{a,b}(N)
\qquad (0\le a,b\le N),
\]
detected on the boundary strip
$\{\Delta_{a,0}(N)\}_{0\le a\le N}$, not another local RTT
calculation.
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Apply Proposition~\ref{prop:completed-target-comparison} with
$\cA_{\le N}=Y_{\le N}$. Since the finite RTT truncation maps are
surjective and the quotients of $\Ydg_{\cA}$ are quasi-isomorphic to
them, the Mittag--Leffler input required there is automatic on
cohomology. The bar-cobar statement then follows from the final part
of Proposition~\ref{prop:completed-target-comparison}, together with
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-standard-mc4-package}.
\end{proof}

\begin{remark}[Application to the H-level identification frontier]
\label{rem:yangian-hlevel-comparison-criterion-application}
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-hlevel-comparison-criterion} is the proved
Yangian half of the frontier conjecture
\ifannalsedition\else
(Conjecture~\ref{conj:master-infinite-generator})
\fi: the remaining step is to supply an RTT-adapted realization of the
canonical H-level target and verify the boundary-strip coefficient
packet.
\end{remark}

\begin{proposition}[Standard type-\texorpdfstring{$A$}{A} realization criterion from shared
bar seed and finite RTT quotients; \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion}
Let $\Ydg_{\cA}$ be a separated complete dg algebra equipped with:
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\roman*)}]
\item a translation operator;
\item a Maurer--Cartan element $r(z)$;
\item a twisted coproduct; and
\item a descending RTT-level filtration by closed dg ideals
 \[
 F^1\Ydg_{\cA} \supset F^2\Ydg_{\cA} \supset \cdots
 \]
 preserved by all three structures above.
\end{enumerate}
Assume further that:
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\roman*)},resume]
\item $\Ydg_{\cA}\cong \varprojlim_N \Ydg_{\cA}/F^{N+1}\Ydg_{\cA}$;
\item for every $N$ there is a dg algebra quasi-isomorphism
 \[
 \Ydg_{\cA}/F^{N+1}\Ydg_{\cA}\xrightarrow{\sim}Y_{\le N}
 \]
 compatible with the RTT truncation tower, standard evaluation
 modules, and the induced degree-$2$ twisting morphism;
\item the quotient tower inherits bar-cobar comparison maps compatible
 with the standard RTT tower and has continuous completed bar and
 cobar differentials; and
\item on the ordered fundamental evaluation line, the degree-$2$
 coefficient is induced by the same ordered bar twisting morphism as
 on the factorization target, in the sense of
 Proposition~\ref{prop:dg-shifted-factorization-shared-seed}.
\end{enumerate}
Then:
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\alph*)}]
\item the filtration on $\Ydg_{\cA}$ is RTT-adapted in the sense of
 Definition~\ref{def:rtt-adapted-filtration};
\item the induced comparison map
 \[
 \Ydg_{\cA}\xrightarrow{\sim}\widehat Y_{\mathrm{RTT}}
 \]
 is a quasi-isomorphism, so $\Ydg_{\cA}$ realizes the H-level
 dg-shifted Yangian target for the standard type-$A$ tower; and
\item the local standard type-$A$ DK-4 packet is already closed, so the
 only remaining Yangian input is the already-isolated spectral
 vector-line realization package; on the multiplicative spectral
 realization locus this is equivalently the standard spectral vector
 seed-and-shift datum.
\end{enumerate}
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
Assumptions~\textup{(v)}--\textup{(vii)} are exactly the hypotheses of
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-hlevel-comparison-criterion}. Therefore the
comparison map
\[
\Ydg_{\cA}\xrightarrow{\sim}\widehat Y_{\mathrm{RTT}}
\]
is a quasi-isomorphism, proving~\textup{(b)}. Since
assumptions~\textup{(i)}--\textup{(vii)} are precisely the data
required in Definition~\ref{def:rtt-adapted-filtration}, this also
proves~\textup{(a)}.

Assumption~\textup{(viii)} is the shared-seed hypothesis of
Proposition~\ref{prop:dg-shifted-factorization-shared-seed}, so the
ordered fundamental degree-$2$ coefficient on the dg-shifted target is
the standard trace-zero Casimir insertion. Corollary~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-dg-local-closure}
then closes the local dg-shifted packet on the standard type-$A$
tower. Thus only the DK-5 categorical packet on the completed
fundamental evaluation modules remains. By
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dg-fundamental-packet-realization},
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-dg-realization-formal}, and
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-dg-packet-ind}, the dg side is already
formal from the canonical completed dg packet and its ind-completion.
Thus the only remaining categorical input is the already-isolated
spectral vector-line realization package; on the multiplicative
spectral realization locus this is equivalently the realization of the
standard spectral vector seed-and-shift datum.
This proves~\textup{(c)}.
\end{proof}

\begin{theorem}[Standard type-\texorpdfstring{$A$}{A} Yangian DK-4/DK-5 closure:
seven variant hypotheses; \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{thm:yangian-dk45-closure-variants}%
\label{thm:yangian-typea-realization-plus-compacts}%
\label{thm:yangian-typea-realization-plus-fundamental-packet}%
\label{thm:yangian-typea-realization-plus-core-realization}%
\label{thm:yangian-formal-moduli-plus-core-realization}%
\label{thm:yangian-typea-realization-plus-dg-packet}%
\label{thm:yangian-canonical-realization-plus-one-seed}%
\label{thm:yangian-canonical-realization-plus-vector-line}%
Under any one of the following seven sets of hypotheses, the standard
type-$A$ Yangian DK-4/DK-5 packet closes.
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\roman*)}]
\item\emph{Realization $+$ compact core.}
 Assume the hypotheses of
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion}. Assume
 further that the compact cores of
 \(\operatorname{Mod}^{\mathrm{comp}}(\Ydg_{\cA})\) and
 \(\operatorname{Rep}^{\mathrm{spec}}(\QGspec(R_{\cA}))^{\mathrm{op}}\)
 are presentable, stable, compactly generated, and exactly equivalent
 in a way compatible with DK-3 on the completed fundamental packet.

\item\emph{Realization $+$ completed fundamental packet.}
 Assume the hypotheses of
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion}. Assume
 further that the completed dg-shifted and spectral categories are
 presentable, stable, and compactly generated; that their compact
 objects are the smallest full stable idempotent-complete braided
 monoidal subcategories containing the completed fundamental
 evaluation packets; and that there exist exact braided monoidal
 functors between those compact cores whose restrictions to the
 completed fundamental evaluation packets recover the DK-3 transport
 and whose composites are the identity on that packet.

\item\emph{Realization $+$ core realization.}
 Assume the hypotheses of
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion}. Assume
 further that the completed dg-shifted and spectral categories are
 presentable, stable, and compactly generated, with compact objects
 exactly $\mathcal{C}_Y^\omega$ and $\mathcal{C}_q^\omega$; and that
 those compact cores are exact braided monoidal realizations of the
 chosen finite-dimensional factorization DK pair in the sense of
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-core-realization}.

\item\emph{Canonical formal-moduli target $+$ core realization.}
 Let $\cA=\mathcal{Y}(\mathfrak{sl}_M)$,
 $\mathfrak{g}_{\cA}:=T_*\mathfrak{F}_{\cA}$ be the canonical
 H-level dg target of
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-canonical-hlevel-target}, and let
 $U^{\mathrm{comp}}(\mathfrak{g}_{\cA})$ be the canonical associative
 dg model of Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-canonical-envelope}.
 Assume that the hypotheses of
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion} hold for
 $U^{\mathrm{comp}}(\mathfrak{g}_{\cA})$. Assume further that the
 completed dg-shifted and spectral categories are presentable, stable,
 and compactly generated, with compact objects exactly
 $\mathcal{C}_{\mathfrak g}^\omega$ and $\mathcal{C}_q^\omega$; and
 that those compact cores are exact braided monoidal realizations of
 a chosen finite-dimensional factorization DK pair in the sense of
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-core-realization}.

\item\emph{Realization $+$ spectral vector-line realization.}
 Assume the hypotheses of
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion}. Assume
 further that the spectral compact core admits an exact braided
 monoidal functor $J_q^\omega$ whose restriction to the vector
 evaluation line is an equivalence onto the completed vector spectral
 line, as in
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-vector-line}.

\item\emph{Canonical target $+$ one canonical spectral seed
 (equivariant multiplicative locus).}
 As in~\textup{(iv)}, let $\cA=\mathcal{Y}(\mathfrak{sl}_M)$ with
 canonical target
 $U^{\mathrm{comp}}(\mathfrak{g}_{\cA})$ satisfying the hypotheses of
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion}. Assume
 further the equivariant multiplicative spectral realization
 hypotheses of
 Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-canonical-realization-to-spectral-seed},
 so that the shift family is intrinsic and the single canonical
 spectral seed $V^\omega(0):=J_q^\omega(V(0))$ is defined.

\item\emph{Canonical target $+$ spectral vector-line realization.}
 As in~\textup{(iv)}, let $\cA=\mathcal{Y}(\mathfrak{sl}_M)$ with
 canonical target
 $U^{\mathrm{comp}}(\mathfrak{g}_{\cA})$ satisfying the hypotheses of
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion}. Assume
 further that the spectral compact core admits an exact braided
 monoidal functor
 \(J_q^\omega\colon
 \operatorname{Fact}_{\Eone}^{\mathrm{fd}}(U_q(\mathfrak{sl}_M))^{\mathrm{op}}
 \longrightarrow \mathcal C_q^\omega\)
 whose restriction to the vector evaluation line is an equivalence
 onto the completed vector spectral line, as in
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-vector-line}.
\end{enumerate}
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
In each variant, Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion}
(applied directly or via its canonical specialization) closes the local
DK-4 packet on the standard type-$A$ tower.

\textup{(i)}
The compact-core equivalence is the input of
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-compact-core}, which closes DK-5.

\textup{(ii)}
The three additional hypotheses are the input of
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-fundamental-packet}, which closes DK-5.

\textup{(iii)}
The compact-core realization is the input of
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-core-realization}, which closes DK-5.

\textup{(iv)}
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-canonical-envelope} identifies the dg
model with the canonical formal-moduli target. The compact-core
hypotheses reduce to variant~\textup{(iii)} with
$\mathcal{C}_Y^\omega$ realized inside
$\operatorname{Mod}^{\mathrm{comp}}(\mathfrak{g}_{\cA})$ as
$\mathcal{C}_{\mathfrak g}^\omega$.

\textup{(v)}
Propositions~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-dg-extension-existence},
\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-dg-realization-formal}, and
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-dg-packet-ind} close the dg side.
On the spectral side, the vector-line hypothesis, together with
the seed-and-shift construction
(Propositions~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-seed-shift-construction}
and~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-core-shifts},
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-seed-realization}), satisfies
the input of Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-core-realization}, so
DK-5 closes.

\textup{(vi)}
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-canonical-realization-to-spectral-seed}
makes the hypotheses of
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-one-seed} automatic. The
completed vector line, fundamental packet, spectral compact core, and
ambient spectral category are all formal, so
variant~\textup{(vii)} is satisfied.

\textup{(vii)}
The vector-line hypothesis is the remaining spectral input of
variant~\textup{(v)} specialized to the canonical target.
\end{proof}

%% ================================================================
%% The seven individual corollaries below are consolidated into
%% Theorem~\ref{thm:yangian-dk45-closure-variants} above.
%% They are retained for reference and for the detailed proofs.
%% ================================================================
\iffalse
\begin{corollary}[Standard type-\texorpdfstring{$A$}{A} DK-4/DK-5 closure from realization
and compact core; \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-typea-realization-plus-compacts-orig}
Assume the hypotheses of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion}. Assume
further that the compact cores of
\[
\operatorname{Mod}^{\mathrm{comp}}(\Ydg_{\cA})
\qquad\text{and}\qquad
\operatorname{Rep}^{\mathrm{spec}}(\QGspec(R_{\cA}))^{\mathrm{op}}
\]
are presentable, stable, compactly generated, and exactly equivalent in
a way compatible with DK-3 on the completed fundamental packet. Then
the standard type-$A$ Yangian DK-4/DK-5 packet closes.

Equivalently, once the H-level dg-shifted realization is constructed on
the shared-bar-seed finite-quotient locus, the only remaining step is
the compact-core equivalence, and that step closes DK-5 formally.
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
By Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion}, the
H-level dg-shifted realization exists and the local standard type-$A$
DK-4 packet is already closed. The additional compact-core hypothesis
is exactly the input of
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-compact-core}, which therefore closes
DK-5. This proves the full DK-4/DK-5 claim.
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[Standard type-\texorpdfstring{$A$}{A} DK-4/DK-5 closure from realization
and completed fundamental packet; \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-typea-realization-plus-fundamental-packet-orig}
Assume the hypotheses of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion}. Assume
further that:
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\roman*)}]
\item the completed dg-shifted and spectral categories are presentable,
 stable, and compactly generated;
\item their compact objects are the smallest full stable
 idempotent-complete braided monoidal subcategories containing the
 completed fundamental evaluation packets; and
\item there exist exact braided monoidal functors between those compact
 cores whose restrictions to the completed fundamental evaluation
 packets recover the DK-3 transport and whose composites are the
 identity on that packet.
\end{enumerate}
Then the standard type-$A$ Yangian DK-4/DK-5 packet closes.

Equivalently, once the shared-bar-seed finite-quotient realization
package is in place, the only remaining categorical step is transport
on the completed fundamental evaluation packet; the compact-core
equivalence and the completed comparison functor are then formal.
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion} supplies the
H-level dg-shifted realization and closes the local standard type-$A$
DK-4 packet. The additional hypotheses are exactly the input of
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-fundamental-packet}, which closes DK-5.
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[Standard type-\texorpdfstring{$A$}{A} DK-4/DK-5 closure from dg-shifted
realization and compact-core realization of a chosen
finite-dimensional factorization DK pair; \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-typea-realization-plus-core-realization-orig}
Assume the hypotheses of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion}. Assume
further that:
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\roman*)}]
\item the completed dg-shifted and spectral categories are presentable,
 stable, and compactly generated, with compact objects exactly
 $\mathcal{C}_Y^\omega$ and $\mathcal{C}_q^\omega$; and
\item those compact cores are exact braided monoidal realizations of
 a chosen finite-dimensional factorization DK pair in the sense of
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-core-realization}.
\end{enumerate}
Then the standard type-$A$ Yangian DK-4/DK-5 packet closes.

Equivalently, once the shared-bar-seed finite-quotient realization
package is in place, the remaining categorical step is to realize the
compact cores as exact braided monoidal completions of a chosen
finite-dimensional factorization DK pair.
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion} supplies the
H-level dg-shifted realization and closes the local standard type-$A$
DK-4 packet. The additional hypotheses are exactly the input of
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-core-realization}, which closes DK-5.
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[Canonical formal-moduli Yangian target closes
DK-4/DK-5 once the compact cores realize a chosen finite-dimensional
DK pair; \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-formal-moduli-plus-core-realization-orig}
Let
\[
\cA=\mathcal{Y}(\mathfrak{sl}_M),
\qquad
\mathfrak{g}_{\cA}:=T_*\mathfrak{F}_{\cA}
\]
be the canonical H-level dg target of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-canonical-hlevel-target}, and let
\[
U^{\mathrm{comp}}(\mathfrak{g}_{\cA})
\]
be the canonical associative dg model of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-canonical-envelope}. Assume that the
hypotheses of Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion}
hold for \(U^{\mathrm{comp}}(\mathfrak{g}_{\cA})\). Assume further
that:
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\roman*)}]
\item the completed dg-shifted and spectral categories are presentable,
 stable, and compactly generated, with compact objects exactly
 $\mathcal{C}_{\mathfrak g}^\omega$ and $\mathcal{C}_q^\omega$; and
\item those compact cores are exact braided monoidal realizations of
 a chosen finite-dimensional factorization DK pair in the sense of
 Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-core-realization}.
\end{enumerate}
Then the standard type-$A$ Yangian DK-4/DK-5 packet closes.

Equivalently, the canonical formal-moduli target already exists. Once
its canonical completed enveloping dg algebra carries the RTT-adapted
finite-quotient/shared-seed package and its compact core is realized as
an exact braided monoidal completion of a chosen finite-dimensional
factorization DK pair, the compact-core DK-5 equivalence and the
completed comparison are formal.
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion} applies to
\(U^{\mathrm{comp}}(\mathfrak{g}_{\cA})\), so this dg algebra model realizes the
standard type-$A$ H-level Yangian target and closes the local DK-4
packet on the canonical formal-moduli target by
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-canonical-envelope}. The additional
hypotheses are exactly the compact-core realization input of
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-typea-realization-plus-core-realization-orig},
with \(\mathcal{C}_Y^\omega\) realized inside
\(\operatorname{Mod}^{\mathrm{comp}}(\mathfrak{g}_{\cA})\) as
\(\mathcal{C}_{\mathfrak g}^\omega\). Therefore DK-5 closes.
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[Standard type-\texorpdfstring{$A$}{A} DK-4/DK-5 closure from spectral
vector-line realization; \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-typea-realization-plus-dg-packet-orig}
Assume the hypotheses of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion}. Assume
further that the spectral compact core admits an exact braided monoidal
functor \(J_q^\omega\) whose restriction to the vector evaluation line
is an equivalence onto the completed vector spectral line, as in
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-vector-line}.
Then the standard type-$A$ Yangian DK-4/DK-5 packet closes.

Equivalently, once the shared-bar-seed finite-quotient realization
package is in place, the dg half of DK-5 is already closed by the
canonical dg compact-core realization and its ind-completion, and the
ambient spectral category is formal from ind-completion of the spectral
compact core.

The only remaining categorical input is therefore the
spectral vector-line realization package; on the multiplicative
spectral realization locus this is equivalently the realization of the
standard spectral vector seed-and-shift datum, and
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-vector-line}
shows that vector-line realization already suffices, and
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-core-from-vector-line}
shows that the compact core itself is then forced as the thick
braided-monoidal closure of that line inside the ambient ordered
factorization category, and
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-ambient-vector-line}
packages the resulting spectral DK-5 closure directly from that ambient
vector-line realization.

While
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-line}
and
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-ambient-one-seed}
and
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-ambient-schur-seed}
sharpen this further to one Schur-simple ambient vector seed together
with the one-parameter trigonometric seed-pair identity on its
dilation orbit, and
Corollary~\ref{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-single-line}
shows that under diagonal \(\mathfrak{sl}_M\)-equivariance and
highest-weight normalization this local packet contracts to one ordered
mixed-tensor line, while on the
equivariant multiplicative spectral realization locus of
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-canonical-realization-to-spectral-seed},
the seed and shift data are intrinsic.
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion} supplies the
H-level dg-shifted realization and closes the local standard type-$A$
DK-4 packet. Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-dg-extension-existence}
constructs the exact braided monoidal dg packet extension
\(J_Y^\omega\), Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-dg-realization-formal}
makes it an equivalence onto the dg compact core, and
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-dg-packet-ind} constructs the ambient dg
module category as the ind-completion of that core. Thus the dg side
already satisfies the dg half of the input of
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-core-realization}. By
Proposition~\ref{prop:quantum-fd-vector-seed-shifts},
Propositions~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-seed-shift-construction}
and~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-core-shifts}, together with
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-seed-realization}, the same is
true on the spectral side with compact core \(\mathcal{C}_q^\omega\);
on the multiplicative spectral realization locus,
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-vector-line}
shows that vector-line realization already supplies the whole spectral
packet, and
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-core-from-vector-line}
constructs the compact core itself as the thick braided-monoidal
closure of that line in the ambient ordered factorization category;
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-ambient-vector-line}
then packages the whole spectral DK-5 side directly from that ambient
vector-line realization;
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-line}
and
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-ambient-one-seed}
and
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-ambient-schur-seed}
show that, more sharply, one Schur-simple ambient vector seed already
supplies the whole object-level ambient route, while
Corollary~\ref{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-trig}
identifies the remaining explicit local comparison there with the
one-parameter trigonometric seed-pair identity on its dilation orbit,
and Corollary~\ref{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-single-line}
shows that under diagonal \(\mathfrak{sl}_M\)-equivariance and
highest-weight normalization this contracts further to one ordered
mixed-tensor line, and
Proposition~\ref{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-exchange}
sharpens that line to one scalar exchange coefficient family;
Corollary~\ref{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-exchange-mult}
shows that this scalar family already descends to the multiplicative
spectral ratio; equivalently,
Proposition~\ref{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-alt-mult}
rewrites it as one antisymmetric-channel character there;
and on the sharper equivariant multiplicative spectral
realization locus,
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-canonical-realization-to-spectral-seed}
removes the seed and shift data as independent choices.
Hence the hypotheses of
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-core-realization} are satisfied, so
DK-5 closes.
\end{proof}
\fi
%% --- end of first \iffalse block (closures i--v) ---

\begin{corollary}[Canonical formal-moduli Yangian target: exact
remaining input after RTT-adapted realization;
\ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-canonical-realization-to-spectral-seed}
Let
\[
\cA=\mathcal{Y}(\mathfrak{sl}_M),
\qquad
\mathfrak{g}_{\cA}:=T_*\mathfrak{F}_{\cA}
\]
be the canonical H-level dg target of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-canonical-hlevel-target}, and let
\[
U^{\mathrm{comp}}(\mathfrak{g}_{\cA})
\]
be its canonical associative dg model of
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-canonical-envelope}. Assume that the
hypotheses of Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion}
hold for \(U^{\mathrm{comp}}(\mathfrak{g}_{\cA})\). Then the canonical
formal-moduli target already carries the standard type-$A$ H-level dg
realization, the local DK-4 packet is closed, and the dg compact-core
side of DK-5 is formal.

Assume further that the spectral compact core \(\mathcal C_q^\omega\)
is realized as a full stable idempotent-complete braided-monoidal
subcategory of
\[
\Factord(\bC^\times;\QGspec(R_{\cA}))
\]
closed under the multiplicative dilations
\(\rho_a(z)=e^a z\), and that the exact braided-monoidal functor
\[
J_q^\omega\colon
\operatorname{Fact}_{\Eone}^{\mathrm{fd}}(U_q(\mathfrak{sl}_M))^{\mathrm{op}}
\longrightarrow
\mathcal C_q^\omega
\]
intertwines the source loop-rotation family
\(\mathsf T_a^{\mathrm{fd}}\) with the target pullback family
\(\rho_a^*\). Define
\[
V^\omega(0):=J_q^\omega(V(0)).
\]
Then the hypotheses of
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-one-seed} are automatic.
Equivalently, on the canonical Yangian target, equivariant
multiplicative spectral realization removes the shift datum and the
base vector seed as independent inputs: the shift family is intrinsic
and the seed is canonical.

Equivalently, on the canonical Yangian target the only remaining
standard type-$A$ input is the spectral vector-line realization
package in the spectral compact core; on the equivariant
multiplicative spectral realization locus, this is equivalently the
realization of the standard spectral vector seed-and-shift datum and
contracts further to the realization functor together with one ambient
compatible
Schur-simple vector seed whose dilation orbit gives the spectral
vector line together with the one-parameter trigonometric seed-pair
identity on that orbit, and under diagonal
\(\mathfrak{sl}_M\)-equivariance and highest-weight normalization even
that local packet contracts first to one ordered mixed-tensor line and
then to one scalar exchange coefficient family.

Once
that ambient seed is placed
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-vector-line}
and Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-core-from-vector-line}
and Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-ambient-vector-line}
and Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-line}
and Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-ambient-one-seed}
and Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-ambient-schur-seed}
and Corollary~\ref{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-trig}
and Corollary~\ref{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-single-line}
and Proposition~\ref{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-exchange}
and Corollary~\ref{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-exchange-mult}
and Proposition~\ref{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-alt-mult}
make the rest formal.
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-typea-realization-criterion} applied to
\(U^{\mathrm{comp}}(\mathfrak{g}_{\cA})\) gives the standard type-$A$
RTT-adapted dg realization, closes the local DK-4 packet, and reduces
the remaining input to the spectral vector-line realization package.
On the equivariant multiplicative spectral realization locus this is
equivalently the standard spectral vector seed-and-shift datum.
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-canonical-envelope} identifies
this dg model with the canonical formal-moduli target.

Under the additional multiplicative-spectral hypothesis,
Proposition~\ref{prop:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-shifts}
constructs the target shift family intrinsically as pullback along the
dilations \(\rho_a\), while the displayed definition makes the base
vector seed canonical. The assumed equivariance of \(J_q^\omega\)
with respect to source loop rotation and target pullback is exactly the
remaining compatibility hypothesis of
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-dk5-spectral-one-seed}. Therefore that
corollary applies and removes any separate seed-and-shift choice on the
canonical target. The final sentence is exactly this reformulation on
the canonical target.
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[Canonical formal-moduli Yangian target: the local
spectral packet contracts to one mixed-tensor line on the equivariant
multiplicative locus; \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-canonical-realization-to-single-line}
Assume the hypotheses of
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-canonical-realization-to-spectral-seed}.
For \(c\in\mathbb C\), define
\[
V^\omega(c):=\rho_c^*V^\omega(0),
\]
and let
\[
\mathsf B_{0,c}^{\omega}\colon
V^\omega(0)\boxtimes V^\omega(c)
\xrightarrow{\sim}
V^\omega(c)\boxtimes V^\omega(0)
\]
be the associated ambient seed-pair braid operator on the realized
spectral compact core. Assume further that for every \(c\in\mathbb C\):
\begin{enumerate}[label=\textup{(\roman*)}]
\item \(\mathsf B_{0,c}^{\omega}\) intertwines the diagonal
 \(\mathfrak{sl}_M\)-action;
\item \(\mathsf B_{0,c}^{\omega}\) agrees with the standard source
 operator on the highest-weight line:
 \[
 \mathsf B_{0,c}^{\omega}(e_1\otimes e_1)
 =
 \mathsf B_{0,c}^{\mathrm{fd}}(e_1\otimes e_1).
 \]
\end{enumerate}
Then the remaining explicit local spectral comparison on the canonical
target is exactly the one-parameter mixed-tensor identity
\[
\mathsf B_{0,c}^{\omega}(e_1\otimes e_2)
=
\mathsf B_{0,c}^{\mathrm{fd}}(e_1\otimes e_2)
\qquad (c\in\mathbb C).
\]

Equivalently, on the equivariant multiplicative spectral realization
locus of the canonical target, once the seed and shift data are
canonical and the diagonal symmetry/highest-weight normalization are in
place, the local spectral packet is no longer a whole trigonometric
family: it contracts to one ordered mixed-tensor line family.
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-canonical-realization-to-spectral-seed}
constructs the canonical seed \(V^\omega(0)\) and the intrinsic shift
family \(\rho_c^*\) on the equivariant multiplicative spectral
realization locus. Therefore the ambient seed-pair operators
\(\mathsf B_{0,c}^{\omega}\) are exactly the operators to which
Corollary~\ref{thm:yangian-dk5-spectral-factorization-seed-single-line}
applies, with \(V^{\mathrm{mult}}(0)=V^\omega(0)\). The two extra
hypotheses here are precisely the diagonal
\(\mathfrak{sl}_M\)-equivariance and highest-weight normalization
hypotheses required there. Hence that corollary identifies the
remaining local spectral comparison with the displayed mixed-tensor
family.
\end{proof}

\begin{corollary}[Canonical formal-moduli Yangian target: the local
spectral packet contracts to one exchange coefficient family on the
equivariant multiplicative locus; \ClaimStatusProvedHere]
\label{cor:yangian-canonical-realization-to-exchange}
Assume the hypotheses of
Corollary~\ref{cor:yangian-canonical-realization-to-single-line}, and
assume \(M\ge 2\). For every \(c\in\mathbb C\), write uniquely
\[
\mathsf B_{0,c}^{\omega}(e_1\otimes e_2)
=
